{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetraccc_a8d9c8ad87fc4c6782c547caf5be61e93}{traccc\+::free\+\_\+indices}} \+: unsigned int}

Components of a free track parameters vector.

To be used to access components by named indices instead of just numbers. This must be a regular {\ttfamily enum} and not a scoped {\ttfamily enum class} to allow implicit conversion to an integer. The enum value are thus visible directly in {\ttfamily namespace \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceActs}{Acts}}} and are prefixed to avoid naming collisions. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\DoxyCodeLine{54             innerAngle = std::atan(xInner / yInner);}
\DoxyCodeLine{55         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 }
\DoxyCodeLine{57         \textcolor{comment}{// evaluating the azimutal deflection including the maximum impact}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58         \textcolor{comment}{// parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetraccc_aab82ddc5db54d9ad84b1215320482993}{scalar}} deltaAngleWithMaxD0 =}
\DoxyCodeLine{60             std::abs(std::asin(grid\_config.impactMax / (rMin)) -\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{61                      std::asin(grid\_config.impactMax / grid\_config.rMax));}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 }
\DoxyCodeLine{63         \textcolor{comment}{// evaluating delta Phi based on the inner and outer angle, and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64         \textcolor{comment}{// azimutal deflection including the maximum impact parameter Divide by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65         \textcolor{comment}{// config.phiBinDeflectionCoverage since we combine}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66         \textcolor{comment}{// config.phiBinDeflectionCoverage number of consecutive phi bins in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67         \textcolor{comment}{// seed making step. So each individual bin should cover}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68         \textcolor{comment}{// 1/config.phiBinDeflectionCoverage of the maximum expected azimutal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69         \textcolor{comment}{// deflection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70         \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetraccc_aab82ddc5db54d9ad84b1215320482993}{scalar}} deltaPhi = (outerAngle -\/ innerAngle + deltaAngleWithMaxD0) /}
\DoxyCodeLine{71                           grid\_config.phiBinDeflectionCoverage;}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 }
\DoxyCodeLine{73         \textcolor{comment}{// sanity check: if the delta phi is equal to or less than zero, we'll}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74         \textcolor{comment}{// be creating an infinite or a negative number of bins, which would be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75         \textcolor{comment}{// bad!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76         \mbox{\hyperlink{inst__nvtx_8cpp_a9fee21184f651ed17410e2a85d0a1f6f}{if}} (deltaPhi <= 0.) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{77             \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} std::domain\_error(}
\DoxyCodeLine{78                 \textcolor{stringliteral}{"Delta phi value is equal to or less than zero, leading to an "}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79                 \textcolor{stringliteral}{"impossible number of bins (negative or infinite)"});}
\DoxyCodeLine{80         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 }
\DoxyCodeLine{82         \textcolor{comment}{// divide 2pi by angle delta to get number of phi-\/bins}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83         \textcolor{comment}{// size is always 2pi even for regions of interest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84         phiBins = std::ceil(2 * M\_PI / deltaPhi);}
\DoxyCodeLine{85         \textcolor{comment}{// need to scale the number of phi bins accordingly to the number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86         \textcolor{comment}{// consecutive phi bins in the seed making step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87         \textcolor{comment}{// Each individual bin should be approximately a fraction (depending on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88         \textcolor{comment}{// this number) of the maximum expected azimutal deflection.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 }
\DoxyCodeLine{91     detray::axis::circular m\_phi\_axis\{phiBins, grid\_config.phiMin,}
\DoxyCodeLine{92                                       grid\_config.phiMax, mr\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 }
\DoxyCodeLine{94     \textcolor{comment}{// TODO: can probably be optimized using smaller z bins}}

std\+::istream\& traccc\+::operator$>$$>$ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::istream \&}]{is,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtraccc_1_1Reals}{Reals}}$<$ scalar\+\_\+t, k\+Size $>$ \&}]{values }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Extract a fixed number of doubles from an input of the form \textquotesingle{}x\+:y\+:z\textquotesingle{}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the values would be separated by whitespace, negative values and additional command line both start with {\ttfamily -\/} and would be undistinguishable. 
\end{DoxyNote}
